style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;-sec-extract:summary;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Item&#160;5.04 Temporary Suspension of Trading Under Registrant&#8217;s Employee Benefit Plans.</span></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br/></span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:4px;text-align:justify;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">As a result of a change in vendors for the McDonald&#8217;s 401k Plan (the &#8220;Plan&#8221;), on November 19, 2019, McDonald&#8217;s Corporation (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) informed participants in the Plan&#160;that they will be&#160;unable,&#160;for a period of time beginning at 2 p.m. Eastern Time on December 24, 2019, to obtain a loan,&#160;withdrawal or distribution from the Plan, and beginning at 4 p.m. Eastern Time on December 30, 2019 to&#160;transfer&#160;or diversify investments or otherwise make investment or contribution changes in their accounts under the Plan (collectively, the &#8220;Blackout Period&#8221;). The&#160;temporary&#160;Blackout Period&#160;for participants under the Plan is expected to end by January 18, 2020. &#160;The Blackout Period applies&#160;to all Plan assets, including Company shares held by the Plan.</span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">On November 25, 2019, the Company provided written notice&#160;(the &#8220;Notice&#8221;)&#160;to its directors and executive officers&#160;informing them of the Blackout Period and the restrictions on trading in&#160;Company common stock&#160;that apply to them during the Blackout Period, pursuant to Section&#160;306(a)&#160;of the Sarbanes-Oxley Act of 2002 and Rule&#160;104 of Regulation BTR&#160;under the Securities Exchange Act of 1934.&#160; A copy of the Notice is attached as Exhibit&#160;99 to this Form&#160;8-K and is incorporated by reference.</span></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:8px;text-align:justify;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">Company stockholders or other interested persons may obtain information about whether the Blackout Period has started or ended, without charge, by contacting the Company&#8217;s Corporate Legal Department by phone at 630-623-3000 or by mail c/o McDonald&#8217;s Corporation, 110 North Carpenter Street, Chicago, IL 60607 during this Blackout Period and for a period of two years after its ending date.</span></div><div 	<body><div style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">
<div><a name="s21301DE8B0D45692AD44A783E90F169C"></a></div><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><div><br></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:right;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 99</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:right;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;color:#231f20;font-weight:bold;">Important Notice to Directors and Executive Officers</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;color:#231f20;font-weight:bold;">Of McDonald&#8217;s Corporation (the &#8220;Company&#8221;)</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;color:#231f20;font-weight:bold;">Concerning Additional Legal Restrictions on Their Personal Trading in Company Stock</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">November 25, 2019</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;color:#231f20;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Federal securities laws require the Company to provide this notice to its Directors and Executive Officers.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;color:#231f20;">In connection with a change in vendors for the Company&#8217;s 401k Plan (the &#8220;401k Plan&#8221;), there will be a temporary blackout period for 401k Plan participants. Beginning on December 24, 2019 at 2 p.m. Eastern Time, 401k Plan participants will not be able to obtain a loan, withdrawal or distribution from the 401k Plan, and beginning on December 31, 2019, participants will not be able to transfer or diversify investments or otherwise make investment or contribution changes in their accounts under the 401k Plan.  These restrictions are expected to end by January 18, 2020 (collectively, the &#8220;Plan Blackout Period&#8221;).  The Plan Blackout Period is required in order to implement a change in the vendor for the 401k Plan, as well as for administrative and technology reasons.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;color:#231f20;">Under federal law, during the Plan Blackout Period, Directors and Executive Officers will be prohibited from directly or indirectly purchasing, selling, or otherwise acquiring, disposing or transferring shares of McDonald's Corporation common stock or derivative securities, acquired in connection with their service as a Director or Executive Officer of McDonald&#8217;s (&#8220;Compensatory Shares&#8221;). These restrictions include indirect transactions by family members, partnerships, corporations, trusts or others involving Compensatory Shares where the Director or Executive Officer has a pecuniary interest. There are limited exceptions to these restrictions (e.g., sales pursuant to court orders or as required by law).</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;color:#231f20;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Please note that during the Plan Blackout Period, the Company&#8217;s trading window will be closed.  As a result, the restrictions referred to above are duplicative of trading prohibitions that already apply to Directors and Executive Officers during this period.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;color:#231f20;">Please contact Denise Horne (by telephone at 630-623-3000 or by mail c/o McDonald&#8217;s Corporation, 110 North Carpenter Street, Chicago, IL 60607) for additional information or if you have any questions regarding the Plan Blackout Period.</font></div><div><br></div><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div>	</div></body>
</html>
</TEXT>
</DOCUMENT>
